Compared with the facilities and equipment, the breakfast on Malta Island is a bit unworthy of the variety, and there is no local specialties. The food time is not up, and many varieties are gone...The equestrian show in the evening is great, and the ticket price is quite expensive. Compared with other domestic parks, I feel that there is not enough publicity and insufficient training of service personnel. The training of the park staff is not carried out, especially the attitude of the security uncles is not very good. And the costumes of the staff are really hard to describe... The last thing I want to complain about is that there are no charging piles in the Maldao basement. The front desk told me that there are no charging piles in the entire park. To charge, I need to go to the nearby Huanghe Supermarket, which is about two kilometers away. I really I'm shocked that there are no charging stations for tourists! Not even a small B&B in the countryside. Does this Pegasus Water City have anything to do with the local power supply bureau? It's really hard to understand...

msg:I traveled during the Mid-Autumn Festival and National Day holidays. I have been admiring Pegasus Water City for a long time, so I stayed at the Maerdao Hotel with my parents this time. The hotel is very good. Robots deliver water and slippers. I stayed for two nights and basically visited Pegasus Water City from beginning to end. There is a musical fountain on one side of the hotel at night, and the art gallery opposite is free and large. You can spend most of the day carefully visiting. There are many exhibits in the exhibition hall. Water must be hidden in the bag otherwise it cannot be brought in. The ticket for the Ma Wenhua Museum is 100 yuan (also 100 for the elderly) and it is worth a visit. On the first night, because we visited too late, the hotel dinner was over, so we ate at Haidilao nearby. On the second night, we had dinner in the hotel's Chinese restaurant. The quantity was large and the price/performance ratio was good. Overall, I was very satisfied.
